KOMORANDUM PC3: CI/0A
ATTENTION
:
SUBJECT
: Traces ca Luis ALEXIC-Souto
201-32969
EXPERENCE
: CI/0A Memorandum dated 15 June 1967
1. Per your referenced request, the FBI documents were located
and reviewed with the fellowine results:
a. The first document dealt with a Luis SOTO who was
appointed Commercial Attache of the Dominican Embassy,
Madrid. This is not our Subject.
b. All documents referenced Luis ALEXI-Souto's
assignment as Cuban Cultural Attache in Mexico City, his
residences, telephone numbers, and his relationships
with the Spanish Communist group in Mexico.
c. The next three items deal with a Luis SOTO, a
member of the FPS of Mexico. This is not our Subject.
2. Subject vas
and his activities
per paragranz 1.b are well known to this Agency. These activities
were considered to be in line with his assignment and are not
presently considered to offer a threat to operational security.
3. PPN Parts I and II will be forwarded your Office upon
receipt from the Station.
Apting Chief, w/1

5 April 1967
AERORANDUM: ROR: CI/OA
ATTENTION:
:
SUBJECT
: LITANTI-9
201-322609
1. LITANTI-9
1. LITANTI-9
1. LITANTI-9
1. LITANTI-9
1. LITANTI-9
2. Since it was believed that LITANTI-9 would have little
4c-
cess to LITANTI or to persons of interest in Mexico, be was terminated
and the balance of his escrow account was paid to him on 9 described
1966. However, it has since become apparent that from time to time
it would be valuable to L'OPACT to contact L'OPACT for information
on FERRECH personalities. He is acquainted with a large number of
persons who themselves are of interest to L'OPACT or who could supply
information on the basis on when information is needed.
3. Therefore, provisions are operational approval and subsequent
operational approval for such national contact with L'OPACT-9 is
requested. It is not planned to pay his a salary or formalise an
agent relationship, L'OPACT-9 would only be contacted when specific
needs for information arise and the possibility exists that he had
or could obtain the information.
Chier, 11/1

MEWORANDUM FOR: C/C1/OA
SUBJECT
:
Operational Approval for LITAMIL-9
1. The Provisional Operational Approval for LITAMIL-9
(C-101331) is due to expire 8 January 1965.
2. In discussions with the field case officer for this
operation, WH/1/Mexico has found that there is no way to
determine when, or whether, LITAMIL-9 will again leave Cuba.
For reasons of personal security, LITAMIL-9 has not been
able to function as a reporting would be to be
Cuba in early 1965. The findings have been his brother, LITAMIL-17,
and are for from occasional Cuban official travelers' transiting
and recindicate that LITAMIL-9 is well and is employed by the
National Cultural Council.
3. LITAMIL-9 is now an inactive agent. The Station
has recently proposed that his salary case accumulating
as of 30 June 1966. If and then again manages to leave
the United States, it is not a kind and a full assessme.t of his
future usefulness will be made. Owing to the fact that his
sister-in-law is a secretary to Fidel Castro it is expected
that he will be a valuable source of information, at le
for an initial debriefing period.
4. It would be appreciated if the POA on LITAMIL-9
could be extended for six months. If at the end of
time he has not left Cuba, it will be proposed that
the
POA be allowed to expire.
W.J. Kafman

19 April 1965
MEMORANDUM FOR: C/CI/OA
SUBJECT
:
Operational Approval for LITAMIL-9
1. An Operational Approval is requested for LITAMIL-9,
who has recently returned to Cuba, and has accepted at FI
mission from Mexico Station. The Station has expressed its
reluctance to interview a Mexican officer who alleged in
1959 that LITAMIL-9 was a Comunist, since this course of
action would unnecessarily draw attention of this officer
to our interest in LITAMIL-9. WH/1 has concurred in this
decision, and considers that this unevaluated derogatory
and
of
a
mance record.
2. Realizing the risk involved in working with any
Cuban national, WH/1 feels that LITAMIL-9's excellent record
of cooperation, plus his acceptance of the idea of continued
and
in
the
of
the
Operational Approval. Additionally, we have had audio
coverage through the telephone in LITAMIL-9's office for
the past two years or more, and during this time the Station
has used the installation for spot checking his information,
and is satisfied that there are no reasons to question his
veracity and security or suspect that he is under control
of the following:
3. Attached for your review are several contact
reports of LITAMIL-9, as requested by Mr. Lally. Their
prompt return will be appreciated. This office will be
pleased to cooperate in any further review of this case
which will facilitate the OA.
W. F. Kayfman
Chief WH/1
Attachments:
Reports of LITAMIL-9

18 November 1963
MEMORANDUM FOR: Chief, WH/3/Mexico
ATTENTION
:
Mike Mulloy
SUBJECT
:
LITAMIL/9
C-101,331
1. Pursuant to a meeting held on 1k November 1963 amongst personnel
of WH/3/lexico, B. Reichart, B. Scott, H. Milloy, J. Manning and of CI/OA,
E. P. Brown and J. Lally, it was agreed that the case of LITAMIL/9 comes
univer the ourview of CSI-F No. 10-5, Section 18a. As such, this
requires
Headquarters approval, i.e. that of WA DIVISION, for the recruimment
a
government official of a denied area country.
2. As described in MEXI-6596, LITAMIL/9 "serves as invaluable eyes
and ears inside target establish the use of an information received
in his face of the proposal was agreed such activity does not require
additional or Operational Approval since LITAMIL/9 is a government of-
ficial of a denied area country. Under these conditions, the processing
of an Operational Approval should not and will not be effected.
3. It was also agreed that if LITAMIL/9 should be employed for cpe-
rational use other than reporting information received in his government
position, the usual Operational Approval or Provisional Operational Ap-
proval procedure will apply.
4. It was agreed that CI/GA would take no further processing action
at this time based on the asove information. However, as in similar
cases, CI/OA will forward to the desu such information made available to
it which might aid the Station in its handling of LITAMIL/9.
Baward Brown
EDWARD P. DROWN
Chief, CI/OA

18 November 1963
MEMORANDUM FOR: Chief, WH/3/Mexico
ATTENTION
:
Mike Mulloy
SUBJECT
:
LITAMIL/9
C-101,331
1. Pursuant to a meeting held on 14 November 1963 amongst personnel
of WH/3/Mexico, B. Fiechart, R. Scott, H. Mulloy, J. Manning and of CI/QA,
E. P. Brown and J. Lally, it was agreed that the case of LITAMIL/9 comes
under the purview of CSI-F No. 16-5, Section 16a. As such, this requires
Headquarters approval, 1.e. that of wa invasion, for the recrundment us a
government official of a denied area country.
2. As described in MEXI-6696, LITAMIL/9 "serves as invaluable eyes
and to be used as a "serving" system of an information received
in his government position. It was agreed such activity does not require
a Provisional or Operational Approval since LIDAMIL/9 is a government of-
ficial of a denied area country. Under these conditions, the processing
of an Operational Approval should not and will not be effected.
3. It was also agreed that if LITAMIL/9 should be employed for op-
rational use other than reporting information received in his government
position, the usual Operational Approval or Provisional Operational Ap-
proval procedure will apply.
4. It was agreed that CI/CA would take no further processing action
at this time based on the above information. However, as in similar
cases, CI/CA will format to the desk such information made available to
it which might aid the Station in its handling of LITAMIL/9.
EDWARD P. RICHIN
Chief, CI/CA

A Provisional Operational Approval is granted for the use of this Subject
as set forth below.
A Provisional Operational Approval issued by CI Staff grants the
authority, on a temporary basis, for the use of an individual as the
granted in as Operational Approval unless otherise specified by CI/OA. It is
based, however, only on preliminary file checks and investigation and
set to a furtier final review when all
FOA is granted only for training of Subject.
Approval for operational use of Subject is deferred pending satisfactori
resolution c: derogatory information, which CI Staff does not consider to
have been accomplished.
To process the Operational Approval, full information (ecepted PRO
Parts I and T:) must be submitted as soon as possible and not later than six
(6) months from this date. An Operational Approval will follow when all
investigation is completed and upon the receipt of satisfactory FRO Parts I
and II. Cancellation must be requested if use of Subject by interested
visions ceases.
